Ababhali nabashicileli bayabonga ukunikwa imvume ngabanikazi bemisebenzi ukuba 
kusetshenziswe imisebenzi yabo kule ncwadi. Kwenziwa konke okusemandleni ukuthola 
bonke abanikazi bemisebenzi futhi abashicileli bangajabula ukuthola imininingwane 
engabasiza ukuze kulungiswe okusele nokungamaphutha uma incwadi isigaywa 
ngokulandelayo.

viii 


INGXENYE YOKU-1 

Ubuciko Bomlomo 
Abantu basendulo babengamaciko amakhulu emkhakheni wokuqamba 
izindaba eziyinganekwane kanye nezinye izinhlobo zobuciko 
njengezibongo, iziphicwaphicwano, izilandelo, amahubo, izaga nezisho 
kanye nokunye. Okuqaphelekayo nokho ukuthi abantu basendulo bona 
babengabubhali phansi lobu buciko ababebuqamba njengoba sekwenziwa 
esikhathini samanje. Lobu buciko babudluliswa ngomlomo ngokwelamana 
kwezizukulwane ngezizukulwane. Lokhu kwakwenza ukuthi ubuciko 
besintu buphile, kuthi nabantu ababusebenzisayo bakhaliphe, ngoba 
phela isimo sasiphoqa ukuthi izindlebe nemiqondo kuhlale kucijile, ukuze 
kukubambisise konke okuxoxwayo nokwenziwayo ukuze kungashabalali 
emiqondweni yabo lokho okulalelwe. 

Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi uma izingane zethelwa (zixoxelwa) inganekwane 
kwakufanele ziyilalelisise ngoba zazingeke ziphinde zilithole ithuba 
lokuzifundela yona ibhalwe phansi. Kanjalo futhi noma kuhutshwa ihubo 
elisha. Lelo hubo elisha kwakufanele lihlale lihutshwa liphindaphindwe 
ukuze lingalibaleki. Nalapho kulalelwe izibongo zenkosi noma zeqhawe 
elithile. Indlela eyayenza ukuthi zingalibaleki, kwakuba ukuzisho njalo 
uma kuvela ithuba. 

Futhi lokhu kwakwenza ukuthi abadala baqikelele ukuthi bahlale 
bexhumene nezingane, ukuze bazifundise lobu buciko, ukwenzela 
ukuthi lolu lwazi lungashabalali kuhle kwamazolo ebona ilanga. Ngaleyo 
ndlela ubuciko bomlomo babuyigugu elikhulu emphakathini, buphila, 
bungagqitshiwe emabhukwini. Singaphawula nokuthi ukungabhalwa 
phansi kobuciko kwakwenza ukuthi bungabi nesimo esisodwa ngoba yilowo 
nalowo muntu wayenegunya lokwengeza aphinde akhiphe amagama athile 
ngenkathi ebusebenzisa. Nakho lokho kwakwenza ukuqambeka kwalobu 
buciko kube wuchungechunge olungapheli. 

1.1 Izinhlobo zobuciko bomlomo 
Ziningi izinhlobo zobuciko bomlomo lapho okungamagugu esizwe 
okwakudluliselwa esizukulwaneni esilandelayo. Le ndlela yokudlulisa 
amagugu yayenziwa ngobuchule obuthile kusetshenziswe amagama 
akhethekile. Bheka nje ngoba kwakuthi kuxoxwa inganekwane kodwa 


ix 


uthole sekungena iculo phakathi naleyo nganekwane. Leli culo laliqukethe 
umlayezo othile . 



Ubuciko bomlomo 

Izinganekwane Izibongo Izithakazelo Amahubo 
Izisho izaga 
iziphicaphicwano 
Izinganeko 
Izinsumansumane 
Umzekeliso 
Ezamakhosi 
Ezamaqhawe 
Ezabaholi 
Izinsumo 

2. Izinganekwane 
Ukuxoxelana ubuciko bomlomo kwakuvala igebe phakathi kwabadala 
nezingane. Izingane zazingalitholi ithuba lokuba zodwa, noma lokuba 
nabantu abangeyiyo ingxenye yomndeni, nabangase bathole ithuba 
lokuhlwanyela imbewu embi ezinganeni. Izinganekwane ziyingxenye 
esemqoka ezinhlotsheni zezindaba ezazixoxwa abantu basendulo. 
Zazixoxelwa izizathu ezahlukene. Phakathi kokunye zazixoxelwa 
ukuthokozisa abanye abangathi ukuchitha isizungu, ukufundisa ngokuthile 

â njengamasiko esizwe, ukudaleka kwezimo nezinto ezithile nokuxwayisa 
ngobungozi bezinto ezithile. 
Isikhathi sokuxoxwa kwezinganekwane yikusihlwa, lapho sekuphele 
yonke imisebenzi yosuku. Kwakuqashelwa kakhulu ukuthi zixoxwe 
kusihlwa, kangangokuthi kwakwesatshiswa ngokuthi uma zixoxwa emini, 
abantu abaxoxelwayo bayomila izimpondo. Yingakho nanamuhla kuthi 
uma kukhona umuntu oxoxa into engakholeki uzwe abantu sebethi phela 
sizomila izimpondo lapha. 

Kukhona umqondo othi igama elithi inganekwane lisuselwa egameni 
elithi ingane noma izingane kanye nokubuza ukuthi âkwaniâ. Kuthiwa 
phela uma kuxoxwa izinganekwane izingane ziba nemibuzo eminingana 
equbukayo, ezizibuza yona ngemiqondo nangolimi lobungane ukuthi 
lokhu okuxoxwayo kungokwani futhi kuchazani. Kwagcina sekuphuma 

x 


igama elithi izinganekwane. 
Izinganekwane zinalezi zimpawu ezilandelayo: 

Isihloko 
Umlandi wenganekwane uyinika isihloko esithile leyo nganekwane 
ayiqambayo. 
Imvamisa isihloko kuba ngumlingiswa noma umdlali osemqoka waleyo 
nganekwane. Kwesinye isikhathi sithinta isigameko esisemqoka saleyo 
nganekwane. 

2.2. Isethulo 
Umlandi uma etha inganekwane uqala ngokuthi kwesukasukela. Lapho 
phela usuke ethula ibika lokuthi sekuyasuka lokho. Izethameli zona 
zikhombisa ukuthi sezikulungele ukulalela ngokuthi ziphendule zithi cosu. 
Lokho-ke umlandi kumtshela ukuthi usengaqhubeka ngoba bakhona 
abamlalele. Nangempela uqhubeka ethule isihloko saleyo nganekwane, 
lapho aveza khona ukuthi inganekwane imayelana nani, kanjena: 

Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Amantombazane ayeyogana indodana yenkosi. 
Ngenkathi umlandi ethula isihloko, usuke ethula yona inganekwane, 
futhi yilapho ezwa khona ukuthi inganekwane yemukeleka kanjani 
ezethamelini zakhe. Phela uthi angasethula isihloko, izethameli ziphendule 
zithi; Sampheka ngogozwana! Uma izethameli ziphendule ngamaphimbo 
aphansi lokho kungasho ukuthi inganekwane isiyisidadada, ngakhoke 
nomlandi wayo akazame amasu okwakha isasasa ezethamelini zakhe. 
Kanjalo futhi noma kunenhlokomo lapho umlandi ethula isihloko, yilapho 
umlandi ezwa khona ukuthi le nganekwane ayethayo iyathokozelwa. Kuhle 
siligcizelele iqhaza elibanjwe yilokhu kuphendulana ngoba phela 
izinganekwane lezi zazixoxwa yizalukazi esezingaboni nakahle emehlweni, 
esezethembela ekulaleleni ngendlebe, nayo eyayihamba ihambe ingabe 
isacosha kahle. 


xi 


2.3. Uhlaka noma isakhiwo
2.3.1. Isakhiwo 
sona siqukethe isethulo: Ingxenye yesethulo 
yiyo leyaya esesihlokweni senganekwane. Kodwa umlandi 
uyaqhubeka-ke futhi ethule inganekwane lapho esengene 
ekuyetheni (ningalibali phela ukuthi ukwetha kusho 
ukuyixoxa) kwangempela. Ngokuvama umlandi uveza ukuthi 
inganekwane yakhe yenzeka kuphi, futhi nini. Ungamuzwa 
ethi, âEzweni elilena kude kwakunenkosi eyayinomusa, 
icebile, inochibidolo womhlambi wezinkomo.â 

2.3.2. Udweshu/inkinga 
Ukuze inganekwane ihlabahlose, kufanele kusheshe 
kwethulwe udweshu noma inkinga. Lapha kubayinoma 
yisiphi isimo esikhomba ukungami kwesimo ngononina. 
Umlandi usengezwakala ethi, âNokho into eyayihlala ihlale 
ikhathaze umoya wenkosi ukuthi yayisikhulile. Kuyihluphake 
ukuthi inkosana yayo eyayisiqinile yayingebukhali 
ngasekuzameni ukuganwa njengontanga bayo.â 

2.3.3. Ukukhuliswa kodweshu 
Umlandi wezinganekwane uyakuqaphela kakhulu ukuthi 
inkinga ayethule ngasekuqaleni kwenganekwane izwakale 
ikhula. Enganekwaneni ethi amantombazane ayeyogana 
indodana yenkosi nje amantombazane abonakala eseduka 
endleleni. Kulokho kweduka intombazane eyiqhalaqhala 
ayinandaba nesalukazi esizama ukuwayalela indlela. Lokhu 
kuyawaphakamisa amaphaphu ezethamelini, zilangazelele 
ukuzwa ukuthi kazi lesi sidididi esesenzeka sizoyiphumelelisa 
yini inhloso yamantombazane. 

2.4. Uvuthondaba 
Inganekwane kufanele idlondlobale iyofika ezingeni eliphakeme 
lapho ingeke isakhula idlondlobale kunalo khona. Enganekwaneni 
yamantombazane ayeyogana inkosazana yenkosi nje, uvuthondaba lulapho 
uZothile esemukelwa efakwa endlunkulu yomuzi wenkosi. Isifiso sokugana 
indodana yenkosi sesifezekile. 

xii 


2.5. Ibohlololo/isisombululo senkinga 
Izinganekwane zivamile ukuba nebohlololo ngoba zisuke zixoxelwa 
izingane. Yingakho kusemqoka ukuveza ukuthi kusala kwenzekeni 
emva kwesigameko esiwuvuthondaba. Lapha ebohlololweni yilapho 
okusuke sekucaciswa ngokuyisifundo senganekwane. Enganekwaneni 
yamantombazane ayeyogana indodana yenkosi nje, kuvela ukuthi 
uMpakana watholwa esemathambo amhlophe ehlathini elimnyama. 

2.6. Amasu okuxoxwa kwenganekwane 
2.6.1. Ukujeqeza emuva 
Leli yisu elisetshenziswa umlandi onekhono lokukhumbuza 
izethameli zakhe ngokuthile asuke esedlule kukho ekwetheni 
inganekwane yakhe. Lokhu usuke enzela ukuxhumanisa 
okuthile nalokho asuke esekuxoxa, kanti futhi kwenye 
inkathi umlandi usebenzisa leli su uma kukhona asuke 
ekhohliwe ukukufaka enganekwaneni yakhe. 

2.6.2. Ukubikezela 
Lokhu kusho isu lokuxoxa ngendlela yokuntshontshela 
izethameli ngalokho okusuke kuzokwenzeka enganekwaneni. 
Isihloko nje singenye indlela yokwenza lokho. Lapha umlandi 
uveza kancane ukuthi yini ezokwenzeka enganekwaneni, 
ngaphandle kokuyixoxa yonke inganekwane. 

2.6.3 Ukuphindaphinda 
Enganekwaneni ukuphindaphinda kusetshenziselwa 
ukugcizelela ubude besenzeko esethulwayo, njengokuthi; 
wahamba wahamba, lokhu kungachaza ukuthi lokhu 
kuhamba kwathatha ibanga elide. 

2.7. Ukuvezwa kwabalingiswa 
Abalingiswa abasemqoka bavezwa ngasekuqaleni kwenganekwane. 
Amagama abalingiswa bezinganekwane avama ukuchaza okuthile ngabo. 
UMpakana uqinise okwempaka. Kanti uZothile uzothe njengegama 
lakhe, futhi uyalalela njengoba bebetsheliwe kwabo. Lokho yikhona 
okumphumelelisayo agcine ekwazile ukugana indodana yenkosi. UMpakana 
ufela ehlathini angangcwatshwa njengegama lakhe impaka eyisilwane. 


xiii 


2.8. Iqhaza lomlandi 
Umlandi wenganekwane uyingxenye enkulu yenganekwane. Uyena 
oyenza ihlabahlose noma ibeduma. Kangangokuthi inganekwane 
eyodwa ingaxoxwa abalandi ababili kodwa yehluke kakhulu ngokuheha 
ezethamelini. Umlandi uyalingisa, aphakamise izwi, aphinde alehlise! 
Abubule, abhovumule! Avule amehlo! Kwesinye isikhathi asukume alingise 
lokho asuke exoxa ngakho. 

2.9. Iqhaza lezethameli 
Izethameli nazo ziyingxenye enkulu ekuxoxweni kwenganekwane. Umlandi 
wenganekwane kuyamsiza ukuziqonda kahle izibukeli zakhe. Lokho 
kumsiza nasekukhetheni iqophelo lenganekwane azoyixoxa. Kuthi noma 
eseyixoxa akhethe namagama azowasebenzisa. Izethameli ziyaphendula 
ezingxenyeni ezithile zenganekwane. Kwesinye isikhathi uzizwa sezibabaza 
uma kukhona okubabazisayo. Zihlahle amehlwana azo uma kukhona 
okwethusayo. 

2.10. Ingqikithi/indikimba 
Ingqikithi yenganekwane yilokho okuqukethwe yinganekwane ngamafuphi. 
Ingqikithi yenganekwane yamantombazane ayeyogana indodana yenkosi 
nje, yinhlonipho. UZothile waphumelela ngoba wahlonipha umyalelo 
ababewunikwe ekhaya kubo. Kanti uMpakana wabulawa ukungalaleli. 
Akawulalelanga umyalelo kanina wokuthi balalele konke abakutshelwa 
umuntu omdala endleleni. Ngaleyo ndlela akasilalelanga isalukazi esasicela 
basikhothe ubhici. Wafa-ke! 

2.11. Umyalezo 
Leyo naleyo nganekwane ivama ukuqukatha umyalezo noma isifundo 
esithile. Phela izinganekwane lezi zaziba yinkundla yokufundisa 
ukuziphatha kahle lapha ezinganeni. Ngakho-ke sivama ukuthola kukhona 
ukushayelelwa kwenkambiso ethile ehambisana nesiko lesizwe. 

2.12. Isizinda 
Isizinda senganekwane simumatha izinto ezintathu. Siqukatha inkathi 
okwenzeka ngayo inganekwane. Siphinde sithinte nendawo okwenzeka 
kuyo inganekwane. Siphinde sithinte inhlalo engamile ngononina ethinta 

xiv 


abalingiswa abathile. Iningi lezinganekwane livama ukuthinta inkathi 
yasemandulo. Ezinye leyo ndulo ziyichaze zithi indala ngendlela engakholeki 
lapho itshe lalisancinzwa ngozipho likhale. Iningi lezinganekwane zivame 
ukukhuluma ngendawo echazwa ngokuthi ezweni elithile elikude. Lokhu 
kuyisu lokuthi ngisho ngabe izethameli azikukholwa lokhu okwethiwa 
enganekwaneni, kuhle zikhumbule ukuthi kwenzeka ezweni elikude, 
hhayi kuleli izethameli ezilaziyo. Isimo sona kuba yilokho okukhomba 
ukungenzeki kwezinto ngendlela ejwayekile. Nakho lokhu kuyisu 
elilungiselela imiqondo yezethameli ukuthi lokhu ezizokuzwa akufani 
nezimo ezejwayelekile. Nangaphezu kwalokho inganekwane iba mnandi 
ngokuxoxa okungejwayelekile. 

Isiphetho esinengwijikhwebu 
Ubumnandi benganekwane bulele ekwethulweni kwesiphetho 
esinengwijikhwebu. Phela leso yileso esiveza okuthile obekungalindelekile 
ukuthi kwenzeke. Emantombazaneni bekungalindeleka nje ukuthi umendo 
uzuzwe uMpakana ngoba ebukeka eyazi indlela eya emzini wenkosi. Futhi 
akayingeni indaba ebhedayo yesalukazi sobhici. Ingwijikhwebu ukuthi 
utholwa esemathambo amhlophe ehlathini. 


Qaphela: 
Sifisa ukugcizelela ukuthi ubumnandi besifundo sezinganekwane 
silele ekuthini umfundi asemukele ngokuzibeka ezingeni lengane 
encane ngokomqondo. Siyomehlula simkhiphe inkani lesi sifundo 
umfundi ofuna ukusibuka ngeso lokuthi yena usemdala nanokuthi 
sikhuluma ngezinto ezingeke zenzeke vele. Sivele sinjalo khona. 
Kodwa izinganekwane zazakhelwe izingane ezincane ezingazibuki 
izinto ngeso ongazibuka ngalo wena mfundi. 
Okufanele kuqashelwe uthisha yilokhu okulandelayo: 
Ubumqoka bemisebenzi yenganekwane. Lokhu kuhlanganisa 
ukuhunyushwa kwenganekwane nobumqoka bayo empilweni 
yansuku zonke. 
Izinhlobo ezahlukene zobuciko bomlomo kufanele zibhekane 
nokukhula kwemiqondo yabafundi njengalena elandelayo: ulwazi 
xv 



lobuciko nezinga lokuqondisisa, ukukwazi ukuhlela kabusha indaba, 
ukusikisela, ukucubungula/ ukuhlunga kanye nokuncoma. 
Kufanele kufakwe nemisebenzana engenziwa ibe yingxenye yokuhlolwa 
okuzinze esikoleni (SBA), njengokucubungula izithakazelo zabafundi 
nokunye okungenziwa ekuhloleni okumiselwe imigomo. 
Ukuhlolwa kwezinganekwane kufanele kufake imibuzo emifishane 
kanye nemide. 
Imibuzo emide kumele ihlanganise izinganekwane, izibongo, izisho 
nezaga neziphicaphicwano okungukuthi kufanele ididiyele zonke 
izinhlotshana zobuciko bomlomo. 
Leli bhuku uthisha limhlinzeke ngezibonelo zemibuzo nezimpendulo 
ngasekugcineni kwalo. 
Ukuchazwa kwezinhlobo zezinganekwane 
Ziyizinhlobo eziningana-ke izinganekwane. Kodwa kunezinsolo zokuthi 
lokhu ukuzidalula ngezinhlobo kulandela ukuzihlela okuthathelwe kwezinye 
izilimi. Endulo inganekwane yayiyinganekwane nje, yehluke ngokuthi 
inandikimba yini. Izinhlobo osekwehlukaniswa ngazo izinganekwane 
yilezi: izinganeko, insumansumane nomzekeliso. 

3.1 Inganeko 
Inganeko yilolo luhlobo lwenganekwane eveza ukudaleka kwezinto noma 
kwesimo esithile. Ngenxa yokuthi ithinta ukudaleka kwezinto, ivama 
ukuthinta noMdali okunguyena odalayo ngokwesintu. Yilokhu kudaleka 
kwezinto nezimo okuphinde kwelule indikimba yenganeko igcine isithinta 
nenkolo. Ingani phela lokhu kuthinta ukuthi isintu sikholwa ukuthi 
ngempela izinto zadaleka njengoba zixoxwa ohlotsheni lwenganekwane 
eyinganeko. 

3.2 Izinganeko zilwane 
Lezi yilezo ezixoxa ngemikhuba ethile yezilwane. Inganekwane kaklebe 
nesikhukhukazi iyisibonelo esihle ngokuveza ukungezwani phakathi 
kukaklebe nezinkukhu. Lezi ziphinde zixoxe ngokuvela kwezici ezithile 
ezilwaneni. Indaba yamagwababa nengulube iyisibonelo esihle salolu hlobo 
ngoba ixoxa ngokuvela kwesipheshula somlomo wengulube. 


3.3 Umzekeliso 
Umzekeliso wuhlobo lwenganekwane olumayelana nomlando othile. 
Kungakhulunywa ngezimpi nezigameko ezithile ezisemlandweni 
wesizwe. Okwenza ukuthi lo mlando wehlele ezingeni lenganekwane 
nokho, wukuthi kusuke kufakwe kuwo okuthile okungakholeki okufuze 
okwenzeka ezinganekwaneni. Kuthi kusalandelwa lowo mlando kuzwakale 
sekukuxoxwa ngezinto ezingakholeki ezifuze ukukhuluma kwezilwane. 
Isibonelo esivelayo somzekeliso esendaba kaNongalaza negwababa. 

3.4 Insumansumane 
Insumansumane wuhlobo lwenganekwane olwakhelwe ukukitaza 
nokujabulisa. Kodwa futhi ziyatholakala izifundo ezithile nakulo lolu 
hlobo. Ziningi izifundo zokuziphatha kwabantu esizithola kulolu hlobo 
lwezinganekwane. Iwuhlobo lwenganekwane oluxube izinhlotshana 
ezahlukene zezinganekwane. Sithola izinganekwane ezihlanganisa abantu 
bodwa; sithole ezinabantu nezilwane; sithole ezinezilwane zodwa, 
ikakhulukazi lezi ezinamaqhinga, okuthiwa ezohlakanyana njengoKhalulu 
unogwaja. Lapha sithola izilwane ezincane zehlula ngokuhlakanipha lezo 
zilwane ezinkulu nezinamandla. Kulolo luhlobo kungena nalezi ezithinta 
ukudaleka kwezici ezithile ezilwaneni kodwa kube kungaveli uMdali 
kuzona. 

3.5 Insumo 
Lolu wuhlobo lwensumansumane olunesifundo esithile esitholakala 
kuyo. Inganekwane yombuso wendlovu iyisibonelo esihle senganekwane 
eyinsumo, ngoba inesifundo. Isifundo sokuzithoba nokungazami ukuthola 
amathuba empilo ngobuqili.

2.4 Ukudaleka kwemidwa ebusweni bengwe 
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela

aqonde ekhaya, angene esebatshazwa, kanti lutho!

Umakadebona wengwe lona wayeyihudula impango yakhe 
eyosithela ehlokozini lezihlahlana elalibuqamamana njena. Kulelo

ngidla kahle nsuku zonke njena!â Esho ebuswa obukhulu ubuvila 
lobu. 


Nangempela umzingeli wahlala lapho intambama yonke elindile. 
Kwathi seliyozilahla kunina, nangempela yasuka ingwe isiyophuza 
emfuleni, iwashiya odwa amawundlu ayo. Wagxuma wahlala 
umzingeli. Into eyafika yamdida ikhanda, kwaba wukubona 
amawundlu esemahle onke ngokwefanayo. Wacosha elokuqala, 



waliphindisela phansi. Wathatha elesibili, nalo wabuye walibeka, 
nelesithathu kanjalo. Ekugcineni wanquma ukuwathatha wonke. 
Ecabanga ukuthi angcono vele amawundlu amathathu kunelilodwa. 
Emva kwesikhashana wabuya unina wamawundlu, washaywa 
yisikhundla sesiqanda njena! Wathi mpu, mpu, mpu! Lutho! 
Wasidinda isililo! Wakhala lokhu okubanga usizi nakozwayo. 
Wakhala kwaze kwakheka imizizima yezinyembezi lapha ngezansi 
kwamehlo. 
Isililo saze sathinta ixhegu elidala lendawo leza lizokhuza umhlola. 
Layizwa-ke indaba ukuthi kanti kukhalwa njena kulahleke 
amawundlu. Lawuhlaba lawulawula endaweni. Kwavela ukuthi 
amawundlu ayethathwe umzingeli oyivila. Waphoqwa ukuthi 
awaphindisele kunina. Yize unina ajabula kakhulu, kepha ayibange 
isasuka imidwa yezinyembezi! 


Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 


Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo:

(d) Iphethwe kahle le nganekwane? (2)

nganekwane, wengeze nangezibonelo zakho. (25)

2.5 Impi yengwenya nendlovu 
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Impi yengwenya nendlovu! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 
Endulo itshe lisancinzwa ngozipho likhale izilwane zonke 
zazihlala ngokuzwana, zizixoxele izindaba zakozilwane. Kuthiwa 
ngalesi sikhathi zazingakawuqali umkhuba wokudlana zodwa. 
Wawungazifica zihleli zihlanganise amakhanda zingqumuza 
izindaba eziyinkinga kulezo zinsuku njengezesomiso 
nezemikhuhlane yazo. Kwenye inkathi uzifice zincomelana 
ngokuhamba kahle kwezinto njengenala yotshani nezithelo. 
Lapho-ke wawungazifica zephula olukhulu uhleko lolu, zihleke 
zize zimbambathane. 
Ngelinye ilanga izilwane ziziphumulele eduze kwesiziba 
esikhulu, ziqeda ukuphuza esizibeni amanzi amtoti, kwavele 
kwasukeleka ingwenya yafaka indlovu umunwe esweni yathi, 
âWendlovu uyazi wena umkhulu ubala njena. Mina ngingakukhipha 
inkani uma kungase kuthiwe asibhekane ngamandla.â

14


âUyazizwa ukuthi uthini kimi wengwenya?â 


âUcabanga ukwenzani ngalokho pho ndlovu?â 

âUyazi ngizokupitshiza ngikukhiphe konke lokhu kwedelela 
mina?â Kusho indlovu kucacela noma ubani ukuthi siyinenga

njena yenziwa nawukuthi ayikaze yayibona indlovu ilwa. Izibonela 
isilima esizilungele njena. 

âManje usancelisa ingane yini ndlovu na?â Kuqhubeka sona

âNawu umuthi engelapha ngawo izichwensi ezifuze wena.â 
Indlovu isho iyicindezela kakhulu ingwenya. Paqupaqu! Ngci! 

Kulokho kushudulisana kwalaba bobabili ingwenya ihlale 
ngamazinyo ekhaleni lendlovu. Ngqi! Nikiniki! Ngqi! Ithi

Ingwenya yazabalaza yayidonsela ngasemanzini indlovu.

nemilenze eyizigwegwe. Kolunye uhlangothi nendlovu yayisinojojo 
lwekhalakazi elide, eselaziwa ngokuthi umboko.

2.6 Ingulube namagwababa
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Ingulube namagwababa! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

Endulo izilwane zisahlala ngokuzwana okukhulu, kwahlasela 
isomiso esikhulu. Kwakuye kubonakale sengathi izulu lihlanganisa

kwesikhashana kubonakale lawo mafu esehlakazekile. Iziziba

yezilwane zibuthise lapho okwakukade kuyiziziba khona,

amanzi khona. Zazilinda umlibe lize liyoshona! Notshani kwase 
kungabakhwekazi! 
âKusho ukuthi lesi somiso sizosibulala sonke wezihlobo zami.â

âSizoke sivuke kusasa siyolunguza ngaleya kwaleziya zintaba.

ngakhona.â Kuphendula igwababa ngendlela eyanika ingulube 
ithenjana. Lisho likhomba izintaba eziyizithunzana le kude. 

âUma ekhona ngempela amanzi, sesiyokuphathela mngani 
wethu ngoba wena awukwazi ukundiza.â

ngakusasa. 

âUma ngilahlwe yinina-ke bangani bami sengobe ngibhubhile.â 
Yizwi okwavalelisa ngalo ingulube ngenkathi sekwehlukanwa.

2.7 UNongalaza negwababa 
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela. 
Izethameli: Cosu. 
Umlandi: UNongalaza negwababa 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwane. 
Kudala ezweni laseNtonteleni elalibuswa yinkosi uMawa, kwake 
kwenzeka isimanga. Lesi sigemegeme senzeka emzini womnumzane 
owayaziwa ngokuthi uNongalaza. Lo mnumzane wayezihlalele 
emthunzini wesihlahla ezishayela umancishana wakhe ethiba 
inhlamvu yelanga elalikhipha umkhovu etsheni. 
UNongalaza wezwa ngezwi lithi, âWeNongalaza, weNongalaza!â 
UNongalaza wathalaza, waqalaza, kepha akabona muntu eduze. 
Emva kwesikhashana wakwedlulisa lokho ezitshela ukuthi hhiya, 
ubezizwela izindlebe zakhe njena. Waqhubeka waziqhabulela 
lapha emancintshaneni wakhe akanganaka nakunaka. Kuthe 
emva kwesikhashana laphinda futhi lelo lizwi, âWeNongalaza! 
WeNongalaza!â 
Kwathi uma esebhekisisa wabona ukuthi leli zwi liphuma 
egwababeni elalihlezi lithe chwa egatsheni lesihlahla ayehlezi 
ngaphansi kwaso. Wathuthumela uNongalaza ebona kwenzeka 
isimanga sento ayegcine ukuyizwa ezinganekwaneni zasendulo, 
ukuthi izinyoni kanye nezinye izilwane zake zakhuluma. Wake wathi 
ukucikica amehlo efuna ukubonisisa ukuthi lokhu ayekubona, 
wayekubona ngempela yini. Nangempela, kwakuyigwababa 
lingaxutshwe nalutho! Futhi kwakusobala ukuthi lalikhuluma naye 
ngoba nakhu lalimbize nangegama lakwabo-ngqo. 
âWeNongalaza! WeNongalaza! Uhlezi awazi nanyaka? Nayi

lazindizela igwababa lansondo.

Abantu-ke abayi nganxanye bengemanzi. Kukhona abathi, hhiya

2.8 Amantombazane ayeyogana indodana 
yenkosi 
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Amantombazane ayeyogana indodana yenkosi! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwane! 
Ezweni elilena kude kwakunenkosi eyayinomusa, icebile, 
inochibidolo womhlambi wezinkomo. Ubisi namasi kwakuyinto 
edlala izingane emzini wale nkosi. Iningi lezingane zase zinonemfu. 
Nenyama yayiphekwa ngomhluzi wenye. Kwakuthi kungonakele 
lutho nje inkosi ivele idumbe inkomo eyithandayo, ithumele 
izinceku zayo ukuthi ziyigingqe. Yayizikhethela kwezinonile 
zodwa izinkomo. Kwakungaba yinkabi, yisithole, yinkomazi,

ngendololwane! 
Nokho into eyayibanga isilalo emoyeni wenkosi ngukuthi

âHhayi bo! Kuthiwe asothatha indlela ejikela kwesokudla uma

âHhayi bo! Ayihambi leyo ndlela wemntanomntanami!â Sisho

kahle indlela engizoniyalela yona.â Pho sisho kubani na! 
UMpakana washaya inqulu yakhe yasho ukuvuthuka epikla ethi, 
âWe! Klibhi klolo! Mina nginguzime oyogana indodana yenkosi, 
angeke ngihambe ngikhothana nobhici lwezalukazi engingazazi 
nakuzazi!â Washo lapho washingila, waziqhubekela ngaleyo ndlela 
ayesezikhethele yona. UZothile bantu yena wasala nesalukazi, 
wenza njengoba isalukazi sasinxusile. Emva kwesikhashana amehlo 
esalukazi aqwebuka, sabona, samyalela kahle indlela uZothile. 

Nebala uZothile wahamba ngokukhawuleza wawelela kuleyo 
ndlela ayeyilayelwe yisalukazi. Ngokushesha wathi esedundubale 



phezulu kwegquma wawubona umuzi wenkosi uyisithabathaba 
laphaya ezansi kokhalo. Kwaba ukufika kwakhe nje inkosi yayalela 
izinceku ukuthi zimngenise endlini enkulu. Inkosi isho nokusho 
ukuthi isimtholile ozogana inkosana. Yayalela ukuthi bajikiswe 
bonke abanye ababesendleleni batshelwe ukuthi sekuqediwe 
ukukhethwa kukazime. 


Kubonakala ukuthi wadliwa yizinunu zehlathi. Nakhona kwase 
kubonakala ngemvunulo yakhe nje ukuthi uyena. Wadabuka 
kakhulu uZothile ngokufa kukadadewabo. 

Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 
Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 
Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 
(a) Ezisuke zinjani izinkomo ezibizwa ngochibidolo? (1) 
(b) Chaza ukuthi ukwenzenjani ukufinya ngendololwane. (1) 
(c) Yini unemfu? (1) 
(d) Kusuke kwenziwani uma kuthiwa umuntu uyothiwa? (1) 
(e) Ukwenzenjani ukuqhawuzela? (1) 
(f) Yini ufasimba? (1) 
(g) Iyini indikimba yale nganekwane? Usho ngani? (4)

Isala kutshelwa sibona ngomopho. Phawula ngalesi simo

chaza nangokuthi yini lo mopho okukhulunywa ngawo lapha na? (25) 

2.9 Indoda neqoma
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Indoda neqoma! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

Komunye umuzi abantu base behlupheke kakhulu yizenzo 
zomuntu okwakucaca ukuthi uyahambahamba. Kwakuyabe 
kuyasa kubonakale izidladla zokubukeka kusamfene egcekeni. 
Kuthi kusabatshazwa lokhu, kubonakale ngobabangibone 
bezinyawo, kucaca njena ukuthi bekugida uqobo lokhokhovu 
lomkhunkuli lapha. Kuthi emva kwezinsukwana kubonakale 
ngezitaputapu ezimnyama ezimpundwini zesibaya sezinkomo. 
Kuthi kusabatshazwa lokho kubonakale impuphu emnyama 
ezindlini, ibhilwe ofindo ngaseminyango yezindlu. 

âHhayi, lokhu sekuphezu kwamandla manjena!â Kukhononda 
umnumzane womuzi. âSekufanele umuntu ayisukumele ayihambele 
le nkinga, kungenjalo lukhulu luzovela kulo muzi maqede yonke 
iminwe ikhombe mina, kuthiwe angilusukemelanga lolu daba.â 
Ngalo lelo langa kwaba sengathi lesi sigilamikhuba sikuzwile 
ukukhononda kukamnumzane. Kwaba sengathi ukuqhubele 
phambili ngokukhononda. Akulalwanga ngalelo langa! Izingcanga 
zazikhonkotha zikhonkothile kuzwakala ukuthi lukhulu zilwa 
nakho lapha phandle. Abanodlebe bezwa umsindo wokubhongisa 
okukafeleba kanohha! Ekuseni abafana belamela izinkomazi 
ezincelisayo zisikeke zasikeka imibele. Nebala kwacaca ukuthi 
kwase kufanele kuthathwe izinyathelo zokulwa nalesi sihlava. 

Ngakusasa umnumzane waphuma kusempondozankomo 
ngenhloso yokuyothungatha ugedla lwenyanga olwaluzomnqandela 
le nkiyankiya yenkinga. Abayaziyo le ndlela ayeyihamba 
babemyalele ugedla lwenyanga eyayikude impela njena nalapho 
ayakhe khona. Njengoba wayephuma ngesokusa nje, ababemyalele 
babehlawumbise ukuthi uma ehamba ekhawuleza, uyofika khona 



zibuya inhlazane. Nangempela kwathi isithunzi singaphansi 
komniniso, wayengena emzini wenyanga. Wathi esakhuleka nje 
kwakuqhamuka udibi lwenyanga luzomngenisa. 


Umnumzane angene-ke kule ndlu. Kushunqa yonke inhlobo 
yezinyamazane lapha! Akubingelelwa lapha. Wathi engena njena 
kwakuhlalwa phezu kodaba inyanga ithi, 

âEwu! Usufikile mnta kaMafikazishintshe?â Kusho inyanga 
imgagula ngegama likayise. Ethuke aqikileke umnumzane. 

âEwu! Bayakuhlupha! Badlala ngomuzi wakho!â Kusho inyanga 
umnumzane engakathi vu belu! 

âEwu! Ehhe! Bathumela onohha bazogida emzini wakho!â 
Kusho ugedla lumgqolozele emehlweni kungazukuthi kukhona 
elukufunda kuwona. 

âBadlala nangemfuyo yakho bayincelisa imikhovu! 
Ubenenhlahla-ke ngoba usufike lapha kithi. Sizoyilungisa le ndaba, 
ehhe! Sizoyilungisa impela!â Akasho lutho njalo umnumzane. 

âEwu, kodwa nawe ulula mfo kaMafikazishintshe! Badlalela 
emzini wakho ngoba sebekubonile ukuthi awuziqinisile 
njengendoda, kanti futhi nomuzi wakho ulula. Ehhe!â Isho manje 
kubonakala ukuthi kukhona ekuphumputhayo lapha ezikhwameni 
zayo. Ikhiphe izimpushana izithululele odengezini imncindise lo 
mnumzane. 

âEwu! Ehhe! Kade wagcina nokuncinda mfo wakithi!â Isho 
igegetheka ngezwi elimahhadla. 



âMfana letha iqoma lami lapha!â Isho ibhekise odibini lwayo. 
âUyabona-ke, lo muntu okuhluphayo uzombona ngamehlo akho 
kusasa lokhu okusayo. Engifuna ukuba ukwenze ukuba uthathe 
leli qoma uhambe nalo. Uthi uma ufika kwakho utshele wonke 
umuntu ukuthi kungaphumeli muntu phandle ebusuku. Ngisho 
kungakhona ofuna ukuyozikhulula, angaphumi! Nawe uqobo 
ungaphumi, ehhe! Ubadonse ngendlebe futhi ukuthi uma kukhona 
umuntu omemeza egcekeni ebusuku bangalokothi bamphendule. 
Nawe futhi ungaphenduli muntu omemeza egcekeni ebusuku, 
ehhe! Kothi kungasa geqe! Uthumele kuyobizwa induna yenkosi 
izobona umhlola. Uqaphele belu ukuthi ningamkhulumisi nhlobo 
umuntu oyobe ebuza okuthile. Wena-ke ozokwenza namuhla 
ukuthi kuthi uma sekulele wonke umuntu uthathe leli qoma 
ulibeke endaweni esobala nje egcekeni, maqede uhambe uyolala.â 
Kwaba njengoba wayelayiwe umnumzane. Wafika wabadonsa 
ngendlebe bonke ukuthi bangalinge baphumele phandle ebusuku. 
Nangempela kwathi kungalala wonke umuzi, waphuma neqoma 
logedla wayolithi chwa endaweni ayeseyihlole kahle ukuthi isobala. 
Kwalalwa-ke.

wenzela ukuthi kube nesiqiniseko sokuthi bayamuzwa bonke 
abantu balapha ekhaya ethi, 


âKodwa ukhona umuntu ongashiya iqoma lakhe elihle kanjena 
egcekeni, lizobhilwa abakhunkuli! Elikabani leli qoma?â

2.10 Isalukazi namasi kamkhwenyana
Umlandi: Kwasukesukela! 
Izetameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Isalukazi namasi kamkhwenyana! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

Kwesukela isalukazi esasivakashele emzini lapho okwakugane 
khona indodakazi yaso yamazibulo. Lesi salukazi safika sibika 
ukuthi sizobalunguza nje izinsukwana, sithi, 

âAngihlezi bantabami, ngizonilunguza njena kwazise kade 
sagcinana.â Kwathi ngokuhamba kwesikhathi sabonakala 
singasayingeni indaba yokuhamba. Kuthi noma umkhwenyana 
waso ephuma nendodakazi beyosebenza emasimini, sizisalele 
emzini wabo. Bothi beqamba bebuya basifice sisazilalele sishaye 
amanhlakomuzi! Undodakazi athi usigoqozela iyambazi, silandule 
sithi, 

âHhayi mntanami, ungazikhathazi ngami. Angazi ukuthi 
kwenzenjani kimi kulezi zinsuku, ngizwa inhliziyo imnyama kabi 
njena.â 

Laphaya endlini engenhla, umkhwenyana wayeseqaphele 
izinsukwana nje impela ukuthi igula lakhe uselelamela lingagcwele 
swi njalo uma ethi uyavuba. 

âYimihlola lena. Leli gula alisagcwali kulezi zinsuku. Kuthi 
uma ligcwele, ngizwe la masi eduma kusengathi anamanzi njena.â 
Ababengakwazi omkhwenyana nendodakazi ukuthi kuba ukusithela 


Â© Copyright: Publishers 



nje uma beya emasimini, kusale kwenzeka izimanga lapha emzini 
wabo. Isalukazi sasiye sintshentshethe siyogila izimanga endlini 
kamkhwenyana. 


âIyangixaka le ndaba yokunyamalala kwamasi ami. 
Okungidida nakakhulu ukuthi nangu nomkhwekazi esecwebezela 
nje impela kulezi zinsuku bo! Kanti ukufika kwakhe laphâ ekhaya 
wayembanjana ziyabalwa.â Ngakolunye uhlangothi indodakazi 
yesalukazi yayisithwe yisithupha nje, ingazi nanyaka. Kuthi 
noma umkhwenyana egudlisela, iphike ngokuthi unina wenziwa 
ukuphatheka kahle laphaya kwayo. 

Umkhwenyana wacupha ugibe lwakhe. Kwathi ngolunye 
usuku wanyomuka laphaya ensimini wanyenya wabuyela ekhaya. 
Wasibona isalukazi esingumkhwekazi sintshentshetha siyongena 
endlini engenhla. Wacathama, wayolunguza. Imihlola azithela 
kuyona yayimangalisa! Sasithe chwa esigqikini sakhe, singazi 
nanyaka. Ukhezo lolu lwalujikijelwa nongakanani umthamo 
emlonyeni! Umkhwenyana kwathi akagxume aphonseke phakathi 
endlini! Nokho kwafika umqondo wokuthi akazibambe ukuze 
abone isiphetho. 

Kwathi sesiya ngasekuwagojeleni amasi akhe isalukazi, 
sasukuma, sagiya. Sigiya nje siyasho nangomlomo sithi, 

âAwuzwe, ngiwakhwelelâ amasi kamkhwenyana, ngidlâ 
indwamba, iyashelela, ngithi chofu, ngithi mimiliti! Indwamba 
ngishelelele!â Lapho-ke wathukuthela wathelwa ngamanzi 
umkhwenyana waphonseka phakathi endlini. Wasiyabula sisathi 
siyagiya! Washo ngembodlongo yezwi elinokucasuka wathi, 

âNgize ngikubambe sonakali ndini! Kanti uwena lona 
oshwabadela igula lami? Unjalo nje awugcini ngamasi ami, uze 
ubhince nemvunulo yami imbala?â Sazithayizela bantu sixolixolisa 
isalukazana. Lapho-ke umkhwenyana kwasekuthi akasiphihlize 
ngewisa sibeyizicucu. Nokho ngoba wayengafuni ukungcolisa 
izandla zakhe ngegazi lomkhwekazi wakhe nokwenza, washesha 
waqhamuka nelinye isu lokusijezisa. 

Wasinikeza isigubhu wathi asihambe siyomkhelela amanzi 



esizibeni esingakhali selesele. Ngokwakhe-ke wayethi wenzela 
ukuthi sihambe singaphinde sibuye. Saphuma-ke sincondile 
isalukazana singasavalelisanga nasendodakazini yaso. Sasithi 
singabona okuyichitshana lamanzi ngisho okunethombonkala, 
kungesiziba, sibuze ukuthi, âKungabe kukhala selesele yini lapha 
na?â Aphendule kube sengathi atshelene amaselesele athi nje, 


Kwathi emva kwezinsuku eziningi, sesihambe sazesalahla 
nethemba, safika esizibeni esikhulu! Saphinde samemeza 
njengenhlalayenza, 

âKungabe kukhala selesele yini lapha na?â Kwavele kwacweba 
nje kulesi siziba. Saphinda isalukazi sibuza ngokujaja, kwaphinda 
kwathula kwathi du! Nebala kwasikhanyela ukuthi yisona-ke 
lesi isiziba esingakhali selesele. Saguqa-ke sawavonxa amanzi 
sawagcwalisa esigujini. Kodwa ngoba sasesikhathele kakhulu 
nelanga likhipha umkhovu etsheni, saphumula emthunzini 
wesihlahla esasiseduze nomfula. Kwedlula izilwane eziningi 
zizophuza kulo mfula. Zonke zazikhuza umhlola zibona lesi 
salukazi esishaye amanhlakomuzi ngaphansi kwesihlahla! Zonke 
zazithi, 

âUbani lona olele ngaphansi kwesihlahla sikaSizemazema? 
Uzombona uSizemazema! Uzomthola uSizemazema!â 

Kushiwo pho lezi zilwane zitshela omunye umuntu. Isalukazi 
sazibuka ubuphoxo lezi zilwane saqhubeka sazilalela. Kwathi 
seliyoshona kwezwakala inhlokomo yezilwane zisho kanyekanye 
zithi, 

âNango-ke uSizemazema, nango-ke uSizemazema!â Zasho 
maqede kwezwakala izigi ezinkulu ziza ngakuso isalukazi. Sathi 
sithi siyasukuma, ngqi! Kanti silele nje sesiboshwe yizimpande 
zesihlahla lesi esasilele ngaphansi kwaso. Sathi sithi xukuxuku, ngqi! 
Zasha! Waqhamuka uSizemazema ukufa kwezintaba! Yizimuzimu! 
Imasaxaba le nto, isho ngezandla ezingakanani! Ikhanda leli 
ungathi elenkunzi yenyathi! Isho ngeso elikhulu elilodwa lapha 
ebunzini! Imilenze lena ungathi iziqu zesihlahla esikhulu! Kwasho 
kwasikhanyela isalukazi ndini ukuthi silibuka siyaligcina namuhla! 



Lapho-ke washo ngelimahhadla uSizemazema wathi, 
âKwanukanuka santungwana!â Nangempela wasibona isalukazana 
siwumfunzana phansi komuthi, sekuphele ubuqha nokuqholosha. 
USizemazema wathi-ke kuhle ayogeza umjuluko wosuku ukuze 
ayidle kahle le nyamazane yakhe ezilethile. Nebala-ke wehlela 
esizibeni esingakhali selesele. Kuwo lowo mnyama kwaqhamuka 
uKhalulu unogwaja egxumagxuma esikhotheni, naye wazithela 
kulesi simo sesalukazi esase sisalelwe yisikhashana sife. 


Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 

Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 


Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 

(a) Ukwenzani ukuvuba? (1) 
(b) Ngonjani umuntu okuthiwa umbanjana ziyabalwa? (1) 
(c) Kushoni ukusithwa yisithupha na? (1) 
(d) Ngonjani umuntu obizwa ngesiphoxo? (1)

2.11 uNananaboselesele noSondonzima
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: UNananaboselesele noSondonzima! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

UNananaboselesele wayevama ukuvuka njalo ekuseni kakhulu 
ashiye izingane zakhe zodwa ayotheza izinkuni, ayokha amanzi, 
ayolima kwenye inkathi ayozingela imbala. Njalo uma ehamba, 
izingane lezi wayezidonsa ngendlebe ukuthi zingalokothi 
ziphumele phandle. Esho ngoba azi ukuthi wakhe eduze nendlela 
lapho okwakwedlula khona izinunu ezincane nezinkulu. Phela 
yena wayengesabi silwane. Akhe endleleni ngabomu ngoba 
eqhoshe ngobuqha nobuqhwaga. Wayesabela zona izingane zakhe 
ezingenziwa isilo sengubo yizilwane uma zizifica zizodwa. 

Langalimbe esahambile uNananaboselesele zadudana izingane 
zaphumela phandle zayodlala. Kwaqhamuka umhlambi wezimfene 
zabuza ukuthi, 

âNingobani nina zingane nibahle kanjena na?â Zaphendula 
kanyekanye zachwaza izingane zathi, 

âSiyizingane zikaNananaboselesele owakhe endleleni ngabomu 
ngoba ethembe ubuqha nobuqhwaga!â Izimfene zanele zezwa 
kuphathwa igama likaNananaboselesele, zenyela, zedlula zihamba 
zibhonga zaze zayosithela ngale kwegquma. 

Ngakusasa futhi esaphumile uNananaboselesele zaphinde zenza 
lokho futhi izingane, zaphuma zayodlala egcekeni. Kwaqhamuka 
umhlambi wezinyathi zama zabuza, 

âNingabaphi nina zingane nibahle kanjena na?â Zaphendula 
izingane ngokwesasa zathi, 

âSingabakaNananaboselesele, owakhe endleleni ngabomu 
ngoba ethembe ubuqha nobuqhwaga!â Kwathi ukuba zizwe 
kuphathwa igama likaNananaboselesele, izinyathi zamisa amashoba 
azo, zagabavula zayosithela egqumeni. 

Nangakusasa zaphinda futhi izingane zikaNananaboselesele 



37 
zaphuma zasakazeka egcekeni ziyodlala. Kulokhu-ke kwaqhamuka 
uSondonzima. Kwandindizela umhlaba, kwasengathi nezulu 
liyaduma, kodwa libalele. Yaqhamuka le nunu ihamba itshikizisa 
umbokokazi wayo. Yathi ukuzibona lezi zingane yama yabuza 
yathi, 
âNgithi ningobani nina zingane nibahle kangaka 
njena na?â Njengenhlalayenza zaphinde zachwaza izingane 
zikaNananaboselesele zathi, 
âSingabakaNananaboselesele, owakhe endleleni ngabomu 
ngoba ethembe ubuqha nobuqhwaga!â Yanele yezwa kuqhayiswa 
ubuqhwaga bukaNananaboselesele yadinwa kabi inunu yathi, 
âNithi niyazi ukuthi nginganimimilita nonke mina kanye naye 
uNananaboselesele wenu lowo?â 
Zachwaza izingane ngokuzethemba zathi, 
âAngeke usimimilite thina, futhi uzomthola uNananaboselesele! 
Thina singabakaNananaboselesele, owakhe endleleni ngabomu 
ngoba ethembe ubuqha nobuqhwaga!â Aziligwinyanga lelo, inunu 
yavele yazihlwitha ngombokokazi wayo yazimimilita, yadishazela 
yazihambela. UNananaboselesele wafika ngetshe lome inhlama 
njena emzini wakhe. Wamemeza kwacishe kwasha izwi, lutho 
ukuqhamuka izingane. Kwavela ijuba elalizihlalele esihlahleni 
elamnyenyezela ukuthi limbonile uSondonzima eginga izingane 
zakhe zonke. 
Akapholisanga maseko uNananaboselesele. Wathatha yona 
Â© Copyright: Publishers 

kanye inyanda yezinkuni, wathatha nesikhuni esasivutha umlilo 
kanye nesinqindi, wangena indlela wabheka lapho okwakuthiwa 
uSondonzima ushone ngakhona. Lapha endleleni wayehamba 
ehuba ihubo ebuza ukuthi uSondonzima lona ushone ngaphi, ethi: 


Lapho liduma lingani, lapho liduma libalele! 

Nebala izilwane ezazimzwela zazimkhombisa ukuthi inunu 
lena ziyibone idishazela ishona ngaphi. Kodwa zazimexwayisa 
ngobungozi bale nunu. Lezo ezazibika ngobungozi 
bukaSondonzima, uNananaboselesele wayeziphendula ngokuthi, 
âAngiyenqeni mina leyo nunu! Mina nginguNananaboselesele! 
Ngakhe endleleni ngabomu ngoba ngethembe ubuqha 
nobuqhwaga!â Asho agqishazele ashone lapho indlovu ekhonjwe 
ngakhona. 

Kwathi esehambe ibanga nje impela, wambona umthakathi 
wezindaba equle ngaphansi kwesihlahla. Waqonda kuye ngqo! 
âWenunu edle abantabami ngithi bakhiphe ubabeke lapha manje 
nje!â USondonzima akachithanga sikhathi, wavele wamumimilita 
nakho konke ayekuphethe uNananaboselesele. 
Kwathi uma uNananaboselesele esengaphakathi kwesisu 
senunu wafica isimanga sento. Kwakukhona inqwaba yabantu 
ababegingwe wuSondonzima. Nezingane zakhe zambona zeza 
kuye sezesese. Akapholisanga maseko uNananaboselesele wabasa 
umlilo ngezinkuni ayeziphethe! Wahhebhula inyama lapha esiswini 
sikaSondonzima ngesinqindi ayesiphethe waphonsa emlilweni 
wosa. Kwadliwa lapha! 

Waqala ukuzibhonqa uSondonzima ezwa ubuhlungu. 

âSengathi ngiginge ishinga lomfazana namhlanje. Yini nginele 
ngimginge lo mfazi maqede ngiphathwe yisisu kanjena?â Yadishazela 
yehlela emfuleni iyophuza amanzi ukwenzela ukudambisa 
lezi zinhlungu ezase ziyiphethe inunu. Yanele yawaphuza nje, 
kwezwakala umsindo wobuhlihlihli lapha esiswini sayo nakhu 
phela amanzi ayesecisha umlilo lona owawulanguka esiswini. 
Kwathi ukuba uNananaboselesele abone umlilo wakhe ucisha, 
wazigalela kakhulu izinkuni eziko. Wavutha ubulangulangu umlilo. 



Kwashunqa intuthu yabheka phezulu. Waphinda wahhebhula enye 
inyama futhi uNananaboselesele, waqinisa nasesibindini manje. 
Kwadliwa! 
Yaqala phansi yabubula yizinhlungu inunu. Yayisizibhonqa 
phansi ikhala ubumayemaye. Ezinye izilwane zamangala zabamba 
ongezansi lapho zibona inunu itabuzela futhi ishunqa intuthu 
ngemuva. Akuthathanga sikhathi yagingqika phansi izibhonqa 
inunu. 


Izingane zikaNananaboselesele zajaja zasho ngengila zithi, 
âSingabakaNananaboselesele, owakhe endleleni ngabomu ngoba 
ethembe ubuqha nobuqhwaga!â 

Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 

Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 


Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 

(a) Yini isinqindi okukhulunywa ngaso kule nganekwane? (1) 
(b) Kuchazani futhi kusukelaphi ukuthi itshe lome inhlama? (1) 
(c) Ucabanga ukuthi yini eyenza ukuthi uNananaboselesele 
aqanjwe leli gama? (2) 
(d) Yini eyasusa udweshu kule nganekwane? (2) 
(e) Yini ekhulisa udweshu kule nganekwane? (2) 
(f) Yini eyingwijikwebu kule nganekwane? (2)

2.12 UGombelakwesakhe nengede inhlava ebizelayo
Umlandi: Kwasukesukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: UGombelakwesakhe nengede inhlava ebizelayo. 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

Endulo kwakwaziwa njena ukuthi uma ubenenhlanhla 
wabizelwa yingede ezinyosini ezinamacwecwe amahle, kufanele 
uthi ungazitapa lezo zinyosi, yona uyishiyele amaqhimu. Uma 
wenzenjalo-ke yayingaphinde ikukhohlwe ingede. Kodwa njalo 
yayikuholela kwezinonile izinyosi lesi. Lesi senzo sasigcwalisa isaga 
esithi ikhotha eyikhothayo, engayikhothi iyayikhahlela nesithi 
izandla ziyagezana. 

Ngelinye ilanga wazibona enenhlanhla enkulu 
uGombelakwesakhe ngenkathi ezithwabazela ehlathini ezwa lokho 
kutshiloza ayekwazi kahle ukuthi okwengede, inhlava ebizelayo. 
Wathi ukuqalaqalaza, nangempela wayibona ingede ithe chwa 
esihlahleni somkhiwane. âNgadla mina kababa! Le ngede noma 
yikanjani ingibizela ezinyosini ezinonile, nokwenza nali nehlobo 
lethwese. Kugcwele umpe nempova lapha ezihlahleni, uju 
lungangobaba.â 

Phela inhlava inekhono elikhulu lokubona izinyosi ezinonile. 
Inkinga yayo njena ukuthi ayikwazi ukuzitapela yona. Ithi 
ingazibona lapho ezivume ngakhona, maqede icinge umuntu 
imkhombise zona. Umuntu olaziyo isiko lokutapa izinyosi 
azikhonjiswe yinhlava uyazi-ke ukuthi kusuke kufanele azitape 
abeseyishiyela nayo. Enzela ukukhombisa ukubonga. 
Nayo-ke inhlava yayihamba ngelikhulu ithemba lokuthi uGombela 
uzokwenza njengoba kwakufanele. 
âNgasizakala mina kababa, ngamthola umuntu ozotapa lezi 
zinyosi, nami angizwise. Futhi ngithole umuntu okahle impela, 
ngoba uphethe izinto zokumba, uzovele azitape khona manjena 
nje.â Kuzicabangela ingede ngokwenama. 



Akuthathanga sikhathi uGombela nengede bedukuza ehlathini. 
Ingede yaye yathi chwa phezu kwesihlekehleke sesihlahla somdoni. 
âHho! Okusho ukuthi lezi zinyosi zakhele kulesi sihlahla. Nansi le 
ngede isihlezi kuso ingasasuki.â Kwaconsa amathe endodeni! Laphoke 
yayisizibona ngeso lengqondo isizivalele elawini layo, isizitika 
ngamacwecwe aconsa uju. Phela uGombela wayengudlayedwa 
woqobo, elifuze akangalishiya leli gama lakhe. Njengoba 
wayeyiphisi njena wayenganqeni nje ukubamba okungumvundla 
akose akushaye akuvale eyedwa khona entabeni. Athi eqambe efika 
ekhaya abike ubumnyama benhliziyo. 

Ngokushesha uGombela wakhetha ukhuni olome kahle, 
walokhela ngomlilo. Waqala wanombela esihlahleni somdoni. 
Waqala wawabona amahalanjonjo ezinyosi eseqala ukundizela 
ngakuye. Phela izinyosi zehlukaniselana imisebenzi. Kukhona 
lezi okuthiwa ngamahalanjonjo. Lezo-ke ngeziyizinhloli. 
Umsebenzi walezi wukuhlola isimo sokuphepha kwesidleke 
kanye nonomthebe wazo. Lezi zinamehlo nezindlebe ezibukhali. 
Uma kukhona okubonakala kuyingozi, ziphuthuma ziyobikela 
amabutho. Amabutho ahlala eduze kwesidleke nangaphakathi 
kwaso. Yiwona-ke atinyelayo. Amabutho ahlale evivela ukutinyela 
konke lokho okubikwe yizinhloli ukuthi kuyingozi. Amabutho 
wona awabonisisi kahle emehlweni, kepha agada okunyakazayo 
nje, atinyele. Kukhona eziyizisebenzi, umsebenzi wazo 
okuwukwakha amacwecwe. La macwecwe asuke engenalutho. 
Ziphinde zizingele uju ezimbalini. Lezi zinamandla, namakhala

bakanomthebe nje kuphela.

ngisho iqhimu elilodwa zwi lapha kuGombela. Kanti ijokola njena

âThemba mphimbo uzogwinya.â Sekusho yena ngenhliziyo. 

Nangempela wayilandela, phakathi, naphakathi ehlathini. 
Kwathi noma eshiywa yigazi ngenxa yokungena engxenyeni 
eminyene kakhulu yehlathi, waziqinisa idolo. Emva kwesikhashana

phezulu! 

Uthe lapho elalelisisa, wezwa kukhona umsindo sakugwavuma

amehlo, maye babo! Uqobo lwayo ingwe! Ufeleba lona ubekade

Kusho ukuthi yilokho okwasindisa uGombela ngoba ukufa lokhu

kwasekumklwebhe kwambeka uphawu ngesidladla lapha ebunzini. 

Zonke izihlobo zikaGombela ziwazi kahle umphumela 
wokungayibongi ingede, inhlava ebizelayo! Indaba ixoxwa 
wuphawu lwesidladla sengwe lapha esiphongweni sakhe. 

Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 
Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu!

2.13 Isigubhu sezinganekwane
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Isigubhu sezinganekwane! 
Izethamel: Sampheka ngogozwana! 

Kulo muzi abazali nezingane zabo ezimbili babehlala ngokuthokoza. 
Abazali babelungile, nezingane zabo zifuze bona ngokulunga 
nangenhlonipho. Babenomuzi omuhle, benanomakhelwane 
abalungile. Kodwa kukhona into eyodwa njena eyayihlupha 
izingane zabo. Leyo nto kwakungukuthi zazingenazo izinganekwane 
ezazikwazi ukuzixoxela ontangayabo uma bethuka bentshontsha 
ukuxoxelana izinganekwane. Zazize zikhamise lapho sezilalele 
amapheqepheqe ontangayabo sebeqeketha ezabo izinganekwane. 
Ezinye izingane zaziye zibatshele ukuthi lezi zindaba zazisuke 
zixoxwa emakubo. Kwenye inkathi zisho ukuthi ezinye 
izinganekwane zazizixoxelwa yizivakashi ezithile ezazivakashile. 

Lapha ekhaya kwakuthuleka njena ngesikhathi sakusihlwa. 
Unina wawumfica ezelukela amacansi akhe, kanti uyise 
wayeqhubeka nokubaza izingqoko zakhe. Le nto yokungazazi 
izinganekwane, yaziphatha kabi lezi zelamani isikhathi eside impela 
njena. Kwathi ngelinye ilanga zagcina zilibhobosile ithumba lapho 
zihleli nonina. 

âMama, yini thina singabinazo izinganekwane lapha ekhaya?â 
Kubuza umfanyana uKhulwana okwakunguyena omdala. 

âEhhe mama, njalo njena thina ezinye izingane ziyasiqinela 
ngokuxoxa izinganekwane. Thina sinoKhulwana sivele singabinazo 
izinganekwane esingazixoxa. OTshengisile sebeyazi ukuthi thina 
asixoxi,â kusho uMncanyana ngokukhathazeka. 

Yamkhathaza le ndaba unina wezingane. Phela akekho umzali 
othanda ukubona izingane zakhe zikhipheka inyumbazana 



kwezinye izingane. Wanquma ukuthi akayethule kusokhaya le 
ndaba. 


âEwu! Kodwa uyangazi njena nawe mama ukuthi angiyena 
umuntu oyisikhulumi. Kanti futhi nakhu nemisebenzi ihlale 
ithe nikilili, sigcina singekho ngempela isikhathi sokuxoxa 
izinganekwane,â kuzibalisela yena usokhaya. Nokho bavumelana 
ngokuthi khona zazikhala ngakhona izingane. Sasikhona isikhala 
sokuhlala ndawonye bewumndeni kusihlwa ngaphambi kokuba 
bayolala. Bavumelana ngokuthi yize babezithanda izingane zabo, 
futhi nazo zibakhonzile, lokhu kungaxoxelani izinganekwane 
kwakwenza ukuthi kube nesizungu laphâ ekhaya. 

Bayixoxa bayixoxa le ndaba, bagcina ngokuvumelana ukuthi 
ubaba wekhaya akaphume uphumo ayohlwaya izinganekwane 
lapha ngaphandle. Unina wezingane wayezosala nezingane 
beqhubeka nemisebenzi yekhaya, balinde usokhaya aze abuye. 
Nebala-ke ngakusasa usokhaya waphuma kusachinsa umthini, 
eseyokwethekela izinganekwane. Esahambe ibangana njena, 
wahlangana nenkawu ibelethe ingane yayo. Abingelele athi, 
âSawubona nkawu. Ngihluphekile lapha. Ungengisize yini 
ungicobelele izinganekwane. Izingane zami zikhathazekile 
ngokuthi asizixoxeli izinganekwane.â Yatshikizisa ugaqasi lomsila 
wayo inkawu yalandula yathi, 

âNgiyaxolisa muntu wabantu, nami anginazo 
izinganekwane ezifanele izingane zakho. Mina engikwaziyo nje, 



Â© Copyright: Publishers

Izwa lokhu kulandula kwenkawu, indoda yedlulela phambili 
yabona ukhozi luhleli esidlekeni salo esikhulu kanye namachwane 
alo amabili. Athathe athi, 

âWelukhozi oluhle, awungisize phela, nakhu ngixakekile. 
Ngihamba ngihlwaya izinganekwane. Umndeni wami 
ukhathazekile ngokuthi laphaya kwami asixoxelani izinganekwane. 
Wena umisa kanjani kowakho, nakhu sengathi nihleli ngokwenama 
njena lapho?â Ukhozi lwathi ukubhula amaphikokazi alo, 
lwathi ukuphakama kwangathi luyandiza lwabuye lwahlala futhi 



esidlekeni lwase luthi, 


Ngokudumala indoda yaqhubekela phambili ihlwaya 
ekuphumele ekhaya. Yahamba yahamba, yazithela phezu 
komhlambi wamadube uklabile. Kwakukhona nancelisayo. 
Nakhona wabingelela wathi, 

âNaze nabahle wemadube bo! Ake ningelekelele phela 
bo! Ngiswele izinganekwane engizozixoxela umndeni wami. 
Kunesikhalo sokuthi asixoxelani izinganekwane kuloya muzi 
wami.â Kubalisa yona indoda njalo. Ezwa lokho, amankonyane 
amadube ake athi ukutshekula, abuya azoncela konina, sekungathi 
ayabukisa. Kwaphendula idube elilodwa lathi, 

âHhawu mntanomuntu, sengathi uhambe kabi lapha kithi. 
Thina phela singamadube. Esikwenza kahle thina ukukhulisa 
la mankonyane ethu. Siyawanakekela, siwancelise siwakhothe 
ukuze kugqame le mibala yawo. Izinkunzi zona ziqalaza lapho 
okuqhamuka ngakhona ingozi, zisexwayise ukuze sibalekele 
endaweni ephephile. Konke lokho ngeke kukusize ngalutho-ke 
wena ngoba awukudingi, ngoba phela uwumuntu!â 

Kwase kuyicacela manjena indoda ukuthi ihlangene nezimbila 
zithutha, ziholwa ngemhlophe phambili lapha. Zonke izilwane 
eyayisahlangane nazo zazingenamgodla wezinganekwane, 
kodwa zaziyitshela ngalokho okuqondene nazo nje kuphela. 
Kuthe isahamba futhi isakhathazekile kanjalo, yahlangana 
nobhejane uhamba nethole lawo. Kwakubukeka kugcwele udaka 



emzimbeni wonke. Kwakulandelwa yizinambuzane njengezibawu

emzimbeni wakho. Yabingelela futhi yathi, 


âIngani mina ngingubhejane nje. Njengoba sihamba sixoxa 
njena naleli thole lami, ngilincomela ngokuphumelela kwesu 
engikade ngilifundisa lona. Phela sisuka obhukwini, lapho 
engikade ngilifundisa khona ngamasu okuzihuqa ngodaka ukuze 
sixoshe izinambuzane ezisihlupha ngokusitinyela. Sixoxa lokho 
nje ukuthi nazi izibawu nezimpukane, azisakwazi ukunamathela 
kithina njengoba sesizihuqe ngodaka njena. Manje lokho wena 
angeke kukwenzele nolunci ngoba awuyena ubhejane,â kusho 
ubhejane uqhubeka udishazela nethole lawo uyoshona lena! 

Zase zehle ngempela izihlathi endodeni ngenkathi izithela 
ekhehleni eselimpunga. Leli khehla lalihlezi eduze nendlela 
lakha isigubhu esincanyana. Lalimatasatasa lithungela isikhumba 
esigujini salo. Yaphinda yabingelela ngokukhathazeka yathi, 
âBaba, awuyilamule bo! Sengihambe lonke izwe leli, ngihambe 
ngithungatha izinganekwane engizozixoxela izingane zami. 
Izingane zami zikhala ngesizungu esidalwa ukuthi asizixoxeli 
izinganekwane. Sengihlangane nezilwane eziningi ngacela ukuthi 
zingisize, kodwa zonke zingibalisela ngokuthi okwazo ezikwaziyo 
akuhlangene nabantu. Ngisize baba!â 

âZiphi zona lezo zingane ndodana?â Sekubuza ikhehla. 
âNjengoba ngisho nje baba, zisekhaya. Ngiphume uphumo 
lokuyohlwaya engizofike ngikwethule kuzona uma sengifika 



ekhaya.â Kuphendula indoda ngokuzilahla. Laphendula 
nekhehla lathi, âNanso-ke inkinga yokuba ngumuntu ndodana, 
wena njengoba uhamba wedwa nje, kanti izilwane azehlukani 
nabantwana bazo.â 


Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 

Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 


Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 

(a) Lichaza ukuthini igama elithi ukucobelela? (2) 
(b) Yini isisusa sodweshu kule nganekwane? (4)

2.14 Ubukhosi bendlovu 
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Ubukhosi bendlovu! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 
Kodukathole bamahlathi, emiphongolweni yezintaba namagquma, 
phansi emajukujukwini emihosha lapho okukhala khona inyoni 
kuphela naphansi ezingoxini zamawa kwakwaziwa nje ukuthi 
kubusa indlovu. Futhi ibusa ngokwethembeka nangokuhlakanipha 
okubonelela zonke izilwane eyayizibusa ngeqiniso. 
Kwakuthi uma isingcifiza ngemilenzekazi yayo, isimpongoloza 
ngomboko wayo, kubone zonke izilwane ukuthi hhiya, yinkosi 
yangempela lena. Kodwa okwakukuhle ngendlovu ekubuseni 
kwayo, ukuthi yayizithobe yedlula iningi lezilwane eyayiziphethe. 
Yize izilwane zaziyikhonzile indlovu, kodwa zikhona ezaziyiphonsela 
inselelo. Ibhubesi nonogwaja njena ngezinye zezilwane ezazithanda 
kabi ukuhlala zihlale, zizame ukuwuphonsela inselelo umbuso 
wendlovu. Pho zizama kubani yena? Indlovu yayivele izibuke njena 
iziqhubekele nokuhola isizwe sezilwane sengathi akonakele lutho. 
Ubuqotho bendlovu babugqama kakhulu uma kunezingxabano 
phakathi kwezilwane. Impi eyayifufusa phakathi kwentibane, 
kanye nobhejane nje yayilamula kalula kabi. Phela izinkunzana lezi 
eziyizintibane, zasukela ubhejane zathi, 
âWena bhejane ayikho indaba lapha kuwe. Thina singakwehlula 
wena ulokhu ulibele ukusindwa yilezi zimpondo zakho zombili.â 
Kwasuka esikhulu isidumo ubhejane esesukela umhlambi 
wezintibane. Okwafike kwaqeda izilwane ezazibukela le mpi 
ngensini, ukuthi kwathi zingasithela nje ngegquma izintibane zathi 
uma ziqalaza zingasawuboni ubhejane zakhohlwa ukuthi zisempini. 
Zaqala zahlwabuya, ezinye zaqala zazinqampunela utshani. Phela 

kuthiwa asikho isilwane esikhohlwa njengentibane, umhlaba 
ungaka nje! Kwathi uma lo msindo ufinyelela endlovini, yazibiza 
yazihlanganisa lezi zilwane yazikhumbuza ukuthi ziyizihlobo 
zegazi. Kusukela lapho aziphindanga zaxabana. 



Â© Copyright: Publishers 



nezinkulu. Kwathi kusuka kwakoma nezihlahlana ezinye izilwane 
ezazisakhalela kuzo ukuze zithole amaqabungana anamanzana. 
Zaqala zakhononda-ke manje izilwane sezithi, 


Kwakhanya nakuyo indlovu ukuthi ayisengangayo, kwazise 
injobo enhle ngethungelwa ebandla! Yabiza ukhukhulelangoqo 
womhlangano wazo zonke izilwane. Kwathi ngosuku lomhlangano, 
yenyukela esidulini sayo eyayigibela kuso njalo uma iphethe 
umhlangano yakhuluma yathi, âBakwethu! Angifuni ukunichithela 
isikhathi! Udaba esihlangene ngalo lapha olokuzama ukuthola 
ikhambi lalesi simo sesomiso! Ngicela sibonisane-ke ukuthi 
kwenziwa njani uma sekunjena. Mina sengihambe ngicinga amanzi 
ngaze ngayobuya lena kude ezintabeni zamanqe, lutho nakhona 
awekho amanzi. Ngicela imibono-ke bakwethu!â 

Ibhubesi libona ithuba lokuketula indlovu esihlalweni 
sobukhosi lasukuma lanikina ikhanda lathi, 

âMina kuyangimangaza ukuthi umholi ozibona efanelwe 
ukubizwa ngenkosi yazo zonke izilwane, sonke lesi sikhathi 
ubengakalicabangi isu lokuthi le nkanankana ingaxazululwa 
kanjani? Kimina lokhu kuyizinkomba zokuthi thina asinankosi, 
sizihlalele nje! Uma kunjena, kusho ukuthi indlovu ayehle 
esihlalweni sobukhosi!â Kwezwakala ihlombe lishaywa yizilwane 
ezimbalwa, phakathi kwazo kukhona nonogwaja. Kulowo mnyama 
kwezwakala ufudu lukhuluma sakuhleba luthi, 

âKodwa mina angiyizwa le nto eshiwo yibhubesi ukuthi 
izoyixazulula kanjani le nkinga yamanzi.â Emva kwalokho 
kwaduma inkwahla, iningi lezilwane lenanela amazwi ofudu. 

Kwaqhamuka nenyathi yabeka amazwi ayehambelana 
nawofudu ithi, 



âNgabe kuyezwakala ukube kuthiwa naleso somiso sidalwe 
yindlovu! Futhi indlovu isicacisele ngemizamo esiyenzile 
yokuzama ukusitholela izindawo ezisenamanzi. Nithi ayenze 
njani indlovu? Akeniyeke ukudlala ngenkosi ngoba izilungele 
bakwethu!â Kwaphinde kwaduma inkwahla futhi emva kwamazwi 
enyathi. Nokho okwakukhanyela noma yisiphi isilwane wukuthi 
lokhu kwenqakisana ngamagama okwakwenziwa yizilwane 
kwakungasondeli nakancane ekuxazululeni inkinga eyayendlalwe 
yindlovu ezilwaneni. 


âMina bakwethu nginalo isu lokuxazulula le nkinga nonke 
esinehlule.â Lapho-ke kwathula kwathi du! Nakhu phela iningi 
lezilwane lalimazela unogwaja ngamaqhinga akhe okuphunyuka 
nasezimeni ezinzima. Kwathi kungathula kanjalo wezwakala 
eseshaya esincane isikhwehlela ethatha ethi, 

âMina bakwethu ngiyamangala ukuthi kungani nonke 
njengoba nilapha njena ningakhumbuli ukuthi kuleso naleso 
silwane kugobhoza imiphongolo ngemiphongolo yamanzi!â 
Kwaqhubeka kwathula kwathi cwaka, kwabonakala zonke izilwane 
zibukana sakubuzana ukuthi kazi uza naziphi ngempela unogwaja 
wezimanga. 

âLawo manzi yilawa ayigazi! Ngakho-ke mina wakonogwaja, 
ngiphakamisa ukuthi yileso naleso silwane asizisike indawana 
encane nje lapho okuzophuma khona igazi bese siphuza lelo gazi 
ukuze sisimame singafi. Uma siphuza igazi, kuzodaleka elinye 
siphinde siliphuze futhi! Kanjalo kanjalo, kuyoze kune izulu 
sikwazi-ke ukuphuza amanzi!â Kwake kwathula kancane, kwaze 
kwezwakala lona ufudu futhi luthi, 

âAngikaze ngiwuzwe-ke umbhedo onjena! Yikhona 
kuhlakanipha-ke okuhlale kubatshazwa kunogwaja lokhu?â 



Kwathi azife yinsini lapho zonke izilwane ezazizwe amazwi 
ofudu. Ezazikude zabonakala zelula imiqala zilunguza ngalapho 
okuqale ngakhona uhleko. Kulezo ezazilunguza kwagqama yona 
indlulamithi ngentamokazi yayo ende. Kulowo mzuzu indlovu 
yayizithulele nje ibuka lesi sidididi, kungazuthi ithi, 


Kwathi kungaphela lelo gidigidi, yathatha indlovu yathi, 
âElami-ke bakwethu lithi asehlele laphaya obekunesiziba esikhulu 
sezimvubu khona. Sifike simbe umgodi ojulile. Yiyona kuphela 
indawo engihlole ngathola ukuthi kungenzeka ukuthi isenawo 
amanzi ngaphansi, esingawathola uma sigubha ngokwanele 
kuyona.â Kwaduma ihlombe emva kwalokho, kwasala lona 
ibhubesi elabonakala lichiza, kubonakala ukuthi uyalicasula lo 
mbono. 

Akupholiswanga maseko-ke kwehlelwa khona esizibeni. 
Kwakuhamba phambili yona indlovu, imba ngawo onke amandla 
ngamazinyokazi ayo. Yayisizwa ubhejane wona owawuqekebula 
amatshe namadwala. Isambane naso sasingazibekile phansi 
sifosha siphindelela ngekhalakazi laso. Nengulube bo, kungakubi 
ukubukela phansi amandla ayo! Zonke nje izilwane zabamba 
iqhaza elibhekile. Lathi liyozilahla kunina kwezwakala inhlokomo 
enkulu lapho sekubonakala amanzi acwebile eqhamuka ekhafuleka, 
ekujuleni komgodi. Kwacacela noma yisiphi isilwane ukuthi isu 
lenkosi enkulu indlovu laba yimpumelelo. 

Kwawelelwa esigabeni esibucayi-ke sokuthi kubekwe 
imithetho yokusetshenziswa komthombo omusha ukuze amanzi 
angaxhaphazeki. Kwaqhamuka lona ibhubesi lathi, 

âThina zilwane ezidla inyama siyashesha ukuzwela ukoma. 
Ngalokho-ke ngiphakamisa ukuthi kube yithina kuqala esinikwa 
ithuba lokuphuza emthonjeniâ¦â Alibange lisakwazi nokuqeda 
lokho elalikusho ibhubesi, zonke izilwane zalihhahhameza 
kanyekanye! Kwagcina sekuqhubeka yona indlovu ithi, 



âBakwethu! Mina ngiphakamisa ukuthi singaphuzi 
emthonjeni noma yinini. Ngoba lokho kuyokwenza ukuthi amanzi 
aphele. Ngalokho-ke amanzi asiwaphuze ekuseni nantambama. 
Singawaphuzi emini kanye nasebusuku. Lokho kuyokwenza 
ukuthi njalo uma sesiyowaphuza siwathole emaningi ngokwanele.â 
Kwaphinda kwaduma elikhulu ihlombe izilwane zenelisekile 
yimibono enokuhlakanipha yomholi wazo oqotho. 


âCha bakithi, ake sibhekane ukuthi yisiphi isilwane esizosithola 
sinodaka. Leso silwane kuyoba yiso esenze lokhu.â Nangempela 
kwabekwa impisi nempungushe ukuthi kube yizo ezibheka 
izidladla nezinselo zezinye. Emva kwesikhashana kwezwakala 
impisi isimemeza ithi, 

âYehheni! yinkosi enodaka ezinyaweni!â Zashaqeka ezinye 
izilwane zizwa lezo zindaba, ngaphandle kwebhubesi elabonakala 
selihleka inhlinini libona izofezeka inhloso yalo yokususa indlovu 
esihlalweni sobukhosi. Phezu kwalesi simo indlovu yona yayibukeka 
ingakhathazekile njena. 

Yathi isuka indlovu yathi, 

âAwuqhubeke mpisi uyobheka laphaya emthonjeni ukuthi 
uzozibona yini izinyawo zami, ubheke nokuthi uzofica ezikabani.â 
Kulowo mzuzu kwezwakala ibhubesi ligwavuma lodwa, likhononda 
ngokuthi, 



âHhayi kuchithwa isikhathi nje manje, kusacingwa kucingwani 
ngoba usetholakele owenze lokhu!â Nokho yaqhubeka impisi yaya 
emthonjeni njengoba yayiyalelwe. Nebala yafica ubunaphanapha 
bezidladla zebhubesi! Indlovu yabeka amazwi ambalwa nje yathi, 


Zasheshe zabona ezinye izilwane ukuthi yibhubesi kanti 
ngempela elenze lobuya bubi. Zabona kabusha futhi ukuthi uboya 
bebhubesi babumanzi bunamanaphanapha odaka. Kwakhula 
ukwethembeka kwendlovu kuzo zonke izilwane, ezincane 
nezinkulu! 

Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 
Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 
Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 
(a) Yisilwane sini intibane kambe? (1) 
(b) Kuchazani ukuthi izinto azimile ngononina? Yini bona 
ononina? (2) 
(c) Yiziphi izilwane ezaseka indlovu? (2) 
(d) Isikhuni sibuya nomkhwezeli. Hlobanisa lesi saga 
nokwenzeka kule nganekwane. (3) 
(e) Ithini indikimba yale nganekwane? (2)

Phawula kabanzi ngalokho esingakufunda ngobuholi bendlovu 
kule nganekwane engenhla. (25) 



2.15 Unogwaja nezingwenya
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Unogwaja nezingwenya! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 


Endulo kwakunamakhosi amabili ayakhelene, kodwa ehlala 
ngokungezwani! Lokhu kungezwani kwakusukela kokhokho 
bawo ababehlala ngokubukana ngeziqu zamehlo. Lawo makhosi 
kwakuyinkosi yezingwenya uNgwenyakazi kanye nenkosi 
yonogwaja uKhalulu. Izingwenya zazihlala esizibeni esikhulukazi 
kanti onogwaja babehlala esikhotheni esiseduze kwesiziba 
nganeno. Kepha kwakuhlale kuconsa amathe kuKhalulu nesizwe 
sakhe sonogwaja uma bebuka amadlelo aluhlaza ayengaphesheya 
kwesiziba. Zaziyima emthumeni-ke kodwa uma becabanga ukuthi 
bangawela kanjani bayozitika ngotshani obuluhlaza ngoba phela 
nazi izitha zabo izingwenya zazixobisile lapha esizibeni. 

Ngelinye ilanga uKhalulu watshela abanye onogwaja ukuthi 
uselicabangile isu lokuwelela ngaphesheya. âSukanini, angeke mina 
ngehlulwe ukwedlula kulezi ziduphunga zezingwenya.â Bababaza 
onogwaja bebona uKhalulu esukela imamba emgodini wayo. 
Kwathi ngakusasa ekuseni ngovivi kwezwakala uKhalulu ememeza 
edelela izingwenya ethi, 

âNina zingwenya niyiziphukuphuku futhi mina Khalulu 
nginganiphatha ngibe yinkosi yenu!â Zathukuthela zagana unwabu 
izingwenya ngenkathi zizwa leyo ndelelo. Okwakuzicasula 
kuzijuqa ukuthi yize babengezwani nonogwaja, yizona ezazinkulu 
futhi zinamandla. Indaba yokwedelelwa unogwaja-ke zazingayizwa 
kwasampela njena! 

âUmthetho wakho wena Khalulu wenziwa yini ukuthi wedelele 
kanjena? Uthi uyazi ukuthi singakuqhobozela khona manje 
wena nalesi sizwana sakho?â Kubuza uNgwenyakazi ngokukhulu 
ukudinwa ezwa la mazwi esigcwaneki esinguKhalulu. 





Kusukela lapho kwacaca ukuthi uKhalulu nesizwe sakhe 
abasophinde basondele esizibeni sezingwenya. Futhi angeke 
baphinde bakwazi ukuwelela emadlelweni ayebonakala eluhlaza 
kahle ngaphesheya kwesiziba. 
waphinde wazisukela izingwenya. 

âWeziphukuphuku zezingwenya, wozani lapha nginikhombise 
ukuthi yimina inkosi enkulu, futhi nginjalo njena mina 
nginobukhosi obukhulu kunobenu!â Kusho uKhalulu. 

âSuka lapha leli phompo! Akukho nogwaja ongabhekana nathi 
thina bakwangwenya, futhi wena akukho bukhosi ogabe ngabo 
lapha! Kungubukhosi yini wena onabo lokhu ugabe ngokuquba 
ezidindini njena?â Kubhavumula uNgwenyakazi. 

Emva kwezinsuku uKhalulu 
obukhulu kunani,

Imibuzo 

Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 

(a) Yini eyisethulo sale nganekwane? (1) 
(b) Umuntu onjani okuthiwa uyiphompo? (1) 
(c) Kungani kuthiwa umuntu othukuthele usuke egane 
unwabu? (1)

(e) Phawula ngengwijikhwebu eyenzeka kule nganekwane? (3) 
(f) Sithola isifundo sini kule nganekwane? (2)

Kwenye inkathi ungakwazi ukusebenzisa izitha zakho ukuze

2.16 Idwi elibusheshelelezi neselesele
Umlandi: Kwesukasukela! 
Izethameli: Cosu! 
Umlandi: Idwi elibusheshelelezi neselesele! 
Izethameli: Sampheka ngogozwana! 


Echibini nasexhaphozini kwakuhlala omakhelwane ababengamathe 
nolimi. Kwakwaziwa nje ukuthi lapho behamba khona nomunye 
ukhona eduze. Labo kwakuyidwi elibushelelezi neselesele elalilihle. 
Idwi lalihlala echibini kanti iselesele lalihlala exhaphozini. Kwakuthi 
uma kubonwa idwi, kwaziwe ukuthi sekuzoqhamuka neselesele. 
Nembala kwakuba njalo. Babebonakala bebhukuda ezizibeni 
kanyekanye. Babonakale bezingela amaqhwagi ndawonye. Ngisho 
nezindaba zokuxinwa amaxina babezixoxelana bobabili. Lapho-ke 
bahleke baze bapansane. 

Kwakungabangani beqiniso laba. Ebumnandini nasebunzimeni 
babemunye. Namzukwana iselesele lisinde ngokulambisa licishe 
linyathelwa yimoto, yidwi elalihambela kuqala liyoliduduza. 
Labeka amazwi enduduzo lathi, 

âYobe mngani wami, khona sekuyoba ngozimakhaza ngoba 
lubukeka lungahlafazekanga lwaphela lolu nyawo, luthintekile 
nje.â Kusho idwi ngelidabukisayo izwi leli. Pho lisho kubani 
ngoba iselesele aliwezwa nalawo mazwi enduduzo, lizibanjelwe 
yizinhlungu nje liqhubeke idwi nenduduzo, âKwankalankala 
njena kuvalwe ngehlahla! Umka nkalankala uthathe wonke 
umndeni wawuweza umgwaqo bethi bayobheka imisundu 
efenyeni elingaphesheya komgwaqo, kanti akabuzanga elangeni! 
Uthe esagudla lukeke ewelisa izingane laqhamuka lingasadle nkobe 
zamuntu iloli lezingodo, lashaya lavala.â 

Ababaze sakuquma uselesele lapho ezwa lezi zindaba 
ezihlasamulisa umzimba. Kusheshe kumcacele ngempela ukuthi 
indaba yokulimala kwakhe ingcono kunalena ayixoxelwa umngani 
wakhe idwi. Abuzabuze athi, 

âUsale wanjani kodwa bantu umnumzane wakhona esesele 
yedwa, ngizwa uthi bekungunkosikazi nezingane?â Lishaye 



Â© Copyright: iStock 

âKanti awuyazi indaba enkulu kangaka mhlobo wami?â Lizame 
ukunikina ikhanda iselesele, nakho lokho kunyakaza kulithunuke, 
liqume yizinhlungu! Liqhubeke idwi lithi, 

âNaye lowo akasekho! Kuthe kungahlatshwa umkhosi 
ngenhlekelele eseyehlele umndeni wakhe waphuthuma eyobheka. 
Ukufika kwakhe nje esibhicongweni, yena-ke wafihlizwa yibhasi 
ebelizedlulela lingazi nanyaka!â Libabazele khona ezinhlungwini 
iselesele. 

Cha-ke baxoxaxoxe bagcine bevumelene ngokuthi abazame 
ukuphelezelana baye ekhehleni lakoselesele ukuze umhlobo lona 
olimele ayothola umhlabelo. Baxhakane-ke batotobele khona 
enyangeni yakoselesele. Osekuthanda ukuhluphahlupha ukuthi 
lapha endleleni sekwenzeka into eyenyelisa iselesele emoyeni phezu 
kwalokhu kulimala kwalo. Izilwane abahlangana nazo zazilokhu 
zibelesele ngokuncoma ubuhle besikhumba sedwi esibushelelezi. 
Kube kusaqhamuke nkomo income, 

âHawu waze wamuhle wedwi bo, ingabe ugeza ngani?â 
Kuqhamuke ngisho umwuzawuza wembongolo, nawo uncome, 

âYehheni lalihle idwi webantu angeke usho ukuthi nalo 
lihlobene neselesele.â Lapho-ke kuthi alizibulale iselesele lansondo 
ukucasuka! 

Bahamba-nje sekukhona nokuzisola eseleseleni ukuthi 
lalivumelani ukungena kulesi simo elalivele lisibona sokujwayelana 
nedwi lilihle kunalo. Bahamba nje akusahambi lona iselesele. 



Kuhlupha khona ukuthi liyaludinga usizo lwedwi. Cha-ke konakale 
kakhulu uma sebefikile enyangeni yakoselesele. Libone iselesele 
ukuthi onakiwe lapha yidwi. Amehlo ogedla lwenyanga lena athe 
njo kophelezelayo. Isiguli lesi isisikhohliwe. Lapho selibitoza 
ungobitoza. Bavalelise-ke! Bahamba-nje sekukukhudlwana 
ukwenyela lapha eseleseleni. Ukwenyela osekuthanda ukuzala 
umona. 


âUzokwelulama umngani wami. Kuphela nje kufanele anciphise 
izindlela ezisondela ngasemgwaqweni ngoba phela kukwawafawafa 
laphaya emgwaqweni.â 

Nebala kwaba alelulamile iselesele. Laqala lazisondeza kakhulu 
emnganini walo idwi. Kwakuyabe uyageza libe lapha, elala libe 
lapha, ebhukuda lilapha, edla libe lapha iselesele. Lingafune 
kuphuthwa yilutho. Linkawuza konke okwenziwa yidwi. Ngendlela 
elalizimisele ngayo ukwefana nedwi, lase liqale nokukhalisa okwalo 
idwi imbala. Inkinga kwaba ukuthi lalisazifanela nje nakuqala. 
Lagcina lizijuba iselesele labuza ukuthi yini lena eyenza idwi 
lithandeke, 
âMngani wami. Zonke izimfihlo zami zaziwa nguwe, nezakho zaziwa 
yimi. Awungitshele phela ukuthi wenza ngani ukuthi isikhumba 
sakho sibe bushelelezi futhi uthandeke kanjena na?â Kungekho 
lutho ngempela idwi elalingakubala ukuthi lenza ngakho, lazithola 
ligwajaza nje alangaphumela obala. Kodwa libona ukuthi umngani 
walo lona uzimisele mawala ukufinyelela eqinisweni labona 
kungcono ukuthi limtshele okuthile okuzomduduza. Ngakho-ke 
lathi, 



âMngani wami, kulula nje. Uthatha amafutha uwafake ebhodweni, 
uwabeke eziko, ubase umlilo omkhulu! Athi angabila amafutha 
lawaâ¦â Iselesele alibange lisalinda nokuthi liqede idwi, labonakala 
libhalakaxela seliyoshona, liqhilika izihlathi ukwenama lisho 
nokusho ukuthi sezixazululekile izinkinga zalo. Nalo lizoke libukwe 
libukeke. 


âAngifune kubonwa muntu, banomona kabi abantu balaphâ 
ekhaya. Uma beke bangibona bangangiphuca nokungiphuca la 
mafutha ami entando. Lisho libhalakaxela liyozivalela endlini! 

Nokushisa kwesitsha lesi esigcwele amafutha akulithenanga 
amandla. Ingani phela laliqinisa ngokuthi impumelelo izuzwa 
ngokwedlula ebunzimeni. Kufike umqonjwana othi okungcono 
akelilinde ukuze amafutha lawa aphole abeyintukuntuku 
okungenani. Kwaphinde kwafika umqondo olitshela ukuthi: 
âHhiya! Yize uvalo ingani lona liyinkunzimalanga lisanda 
kuphulukundlela lasinda linyathelwa yimoto, abeyini amafutha 
lawa!â 

Lasho lazibhunyela ngamafutha! Lwasuka uthuli lwezichwe! 
Ukushiswa amafutha-ke kuyahlupha ngoba wona ayanamathela 
emzimbeni! Awafani namanzi wona azigingqikela kalula 
emzimbeni engakawenzi umonakalo omkhulu. Ukuthi isicabha 
lasikhahlela kanjani, akwaziwa! Okwaziwayo ukuthi laphuma 
lampampa lagcwala igceke iselesele! Bathi bayaliphuthuma lapha 
egcekeni lezwakala selikloloba phakathi exhaphozini elisezansana 
komuzi walo! 



Kwathi ingathi damu iminjunju yokuzipheka ngamafutha, 
lalifutheka lenyukela emzini wedwi. Lapho selinjani! Limapanyaza 
wukushiswa ngamafutha. Liyaxhutha! Isikhumba lesi ebesingethusi 
sesiphenduke samaholoholo. Ubuhle balo bemvelo abusabonwa 
ndawo. Lifutheka nje liphethe isiceshana samafutha ayesale 
ebhodweni. Inye inhloso. Yimpindiselo! Sisole nokho isalukazi 
ukuthi lo osenjena, nalokhuya kubhalakaxela akunabulungiswa, 
ikhona impi eyosuswa phambili, maqede isalukazi silibeke 
ezithendeni iselesele. Lathi liyongena emzini wedwi, nesalukazi sase 
silapha! Nakuba kuyakhulunywa ukuthi laqala lakhuluma iselesele, 
lase lenzela sona isalukazi leso ukuthi sizwe ukuthi kungani isimo 
sinjena. 


âHawu sekwenzenjani kodwa mngani wami, ushiswe yini 
kanjena na?â Lapho-ke libhoke likhahlele iselesele. Ingani phela 
sekuyalicacela ukuthi lo mnganyana mbumbulu ubelenza isiwula 
sonke lesi sikhathi. 

âUngenza isilima, uthi angibilise amafutha ngizithele ngawo! 
Ubufuna ngibe njena angithi? Usuyajabula-ke?â Lisho limsikaza 
ngesitsha eliphethe ngaso amafutha abukeka esashisa impela nje! 
Kuleso sidididi kutheleke isalukazi seselesele esasithi siyalamula! 
Sikhale uqanduqandu isalukazi sansondo! 

Isixongololo somsindo laphaya emzini wedwi sasesibuthele 
ndawonye bonke omakhelwane. Kwase kufike nenduna enkulu 
indlovu. Kwathiwa aliqale ekuqaleni lichaze idwi ukuthi lo 
monakalo uqalephi. Liqale-ke ngokudangala idwi lenkosi lithi, 

âWena wakomkhulu nomphakathi womakhelwane, umngani 
wami lona osenjena namuhla wangibuza ukuthi ngisenza ngani 
isikhumba sami ukuthi sibe bushelelezi kanjena na. Nami-ke 
kwakungekho nanto engangingathi ngenza ngayo. Kodwa ngase 
ngenzela ukuthi aneliseke nje ngoba esengixine isikhathi eside 
engibuza, ngabona kungcono ngimtshele isu lokwakha amafutha 
okugcoba emzimbeni engiye ngiwasebenzise.â 

âNgamtshela-ke uselesele ukuthi kufanele abase umlilo 



omkhulu. Athathe amafutha amaningi awafake ebhodweni, 
alibeke eziko, maqede awalinde abile amafutha. Kodwa kwathi 
ngingakaqedi wavele wazishaya umuntu owaziyo ukuthi 
kwenziwani, emva kwalokho, wavalelisa wahamba. Kanti mina 
bengisazosho ukuthi uma amafutha esebila uyawephula eziko. 
Kothi angaphola uwathululele ezitsheni ezincane. Usengalokhu 
ewagcoba-ke la mafutha njalo emva kokugeza. Ngiyamangala njena 
uma sengimbona esenjena!â Zababaza zonke izilwane ezazilalele! 
âKunjalo ngempela selesele?â kubuza induna indlovu. 
âYebo nkosi yezilwaneâ kusho iselesele ngamahlonyana. 
Lungasabonwa ulaka elalifike nalo. 


Umlandi: Cosucosu iyaphela! 

Izethameli: Siyabonga imnandi kakhulu! 

Imibuzo 


Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo: 

(a) Yini ixina? (1) 
(b) Kusho ukwenzani ukunkawuza into? (1) 
(c) Idwi neselesele abangabalingiswa lapha, babebulili buni? 
Ukusho ngani lokho? (2) 
(d) Nika incazelo nemvelaphi yesisho esithi ukusinda 
ngokulambisa. (2) 
(e) Sithini isifundo esisemqoka sale nganekwane na? (2) 
(f) âUmona usuka esweni.â Phawula ngalesi saga, kuhambisane 
nale nganekwane. (2) 

Umbuzo omude 

Ususela kule nganekwane yedwi neselesele, xoxa ngendaba eseyake 
yakwehlela noma osewake wayibona noma wezwa ngayo eyehlela 
abantu abangabangani. Bagcina sebexabene ngendlela eyefuze lena. (25)
